 12 varsh se kam tathaa 65 varsh se adhik umr varg ke logon ko tathaa vyapaariyon ko police reporting se chhot nae samjhaute kii khaasiyaton main shaamil he
 This visa agreement has come into force at a time when the pakistan-india cricket series is going to take place

 Senior plays an important role in every office
 kyonki senior ko dekhakar hi unke juniurs ko kaam karne kii motiveshan milti he
 If after this appraisal you have got the post of senior, then how can you become a perfect senior in front of your juniors, definitely know this
 
 
 galtiyaan sudhaarney ke liye rahen taiyaarakyonki senior bhi kabhi junior tha
 
 
 Always remember this thing
 aapkaa junior agar galtiyaan kare to use is baat kaa vishwaas dilaaein ki aap khadey hai unki galtiyaan sudhaarney ke liye
 When the team gives good performance, then boost the team in this way
 
 
 guide karte rahenek cheez hameshaa yaad rakhen ki aapke juniurs aapaki jimmedaari hai
 How much better they will do in future depends on your guidance
 isliye acha kaam kaise karnaa he iske liye unhen guide karte rahen
 Understand what is the problem in their problem office, even if they are unable to share with you
 par aapkaa haq he ki aap unki problem ko samajhen
 It is not just the work of a senior to get work report and work done
 jab bos kaa chillaanaa ban jaae daily routine, to yun rakhen khud ko kulkam ko badhawadeshgar aapkaa junior apane kaam ko impruva karne kii koshish kar rahaa he yaa phir nae idia aapke saamne rakh rahaa he to unke idia kii tariff karen
 By doing this, self-confidence will grow in them
 comfortable feel karaayenkam ko lekar aap syriasnes barat rahen he, ye thik he
 But it is not right to always be serious
 juniurs ke saath thodaa hansi-majaak kar aap unhen comfortable feel kara sakate hai
 Do not shout in front of everyone
 jaahir si baat he galtiyaan karegaa
 But even if he makes a mistake, you should explain it in private by not scolding everyone
 agar aap sabake saamne daantenge to shaayad unhen sharmindagi mahasoos ho
 Which can divert their focus from work
 bejaan offis desk main yun bharen jaan
 
 
 Give freedom to work
 Everyone's style of working is different
 jaahir si baat he unka bhi tarika alag hoga
 So when they work, leave them free
 phir dekhie, kaise creativity baahar nikalati he
 Explain that if their focus is removed on the importance of work, then from time to time, keep explaining the importance of work
 kyonki aaj nahin to kal wo bhi junior se senior ban hi jaaenge
